</header><div class="entry-content"><div class="tasty-pins-hidden-image-container" style="display:none;"><img alt="Big pot of our Tuscan Beef and Lentil Soup recipe" class="tasty-pins-hidden-image" data-pin-description="COZY Tuscan-Style Beef &amp; Lentil Soup. 1 pot, simple ingredients, quick, SO satisfying. <p>If you’re looking for a <strong>hearty, 1-pot meal</strong> to warm up with this winter, this is it.</p>
<p>I recently got an intense craving for a <strong>meaty, tomatoey soup with lentils and greens</strong> and <em>had</em> to have it. This was the (incredibly delicious) result. </p>
<p>We hope you love it as much as we do. It’s been on repeat in our kitchen for the last several months! Let us show you how easily it comes together.</p>
<iframe allow="accelerometer; autoplay; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture" allowfullscreen="" frameborder="0" height="380" src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/dgmZUnfplM8" width="680"></iframe>
<figure class="wp-block-image"><img alt="Kale, lentils, tomatoes, herbs, onion, garlic, salt, and ground beef for making our Tuscan-Style Beef &amp; Lentil Soup." class="wp-image-50268" data-jpibfi-post-excerpt="" data-jpibfi-post-title="1-Pot Tuscan-Style Beef &amp; Lentil Soup" data-jpibfi-post-url="https://minimalistbaker.com/1-pot-tuscan-style-beef-lentil-soup/" data-jpibfi-src="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/12/COZY-Tuscan-Style-Beef-Lentil-Soup.-1-pot-simple-ingredients-quick-SO-satisfying.-Vegan-options.-minimalistbaker-lentils-glutenfree-soup-recipe.jpg" data-pin-description="COZY Tuscan-Style Beef &amp; Lentil Soup. 1 pot, simple ingredients, quick, SO satisfying. <span id="more-50243"></span>
<p>This 1-pot soup starts with sautéing onion and garlic. Red pepper flake adds a little heat, which is optional but recommended.</p>
<p>Next comes the meat. We’ve tested this recipe with lean ground beef, bison, and even some nice quality pork sausage, and all worked well. Our favorites, however, are beef and bison (vegan options below, too).</p>
<figure class="wp-block-image"><img alt="Stirring the ground beef and tomatoes for our Tuscan-Style Beef &amp; Lentil Soup recipe" class="wp-image-50251" data-jpibfi-post-excerpt="" data-jpibfi-post-title="1-Pot Tuscan-Style Beef &amp; Lentil Soup" data-jpibfi-post-url="https://minimalistbaker.com/1-pot-tuscan-style-beef-lentil-soup/" data-jpibfi-src="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/12/COZY-Tuscan-Style-Beef-Lentil-Soup.-1-pot-simple-ingredients-quick-SO-satisfying.-Vegan-options.-minimalistbaker-lentils-glutenfree-soup-recipe-4.jpg" data-pin-description="COZY Tuscan-Style Beef &amp; Lentil Soup. 1 pot, simple ingredients, quick, SO satisfying. Vegan options. #minimalistbaker #lentils #glutenfree #soup #recipe" data-pin-title="1-Pot Tuscan-Style Beef &amp; Lentil Soup" sizes="(max-width: 960px) 100vw, (max-width: 1149px) 590px, 720px" src="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/12/COZY-Tuscan-Style-Beef-Lentil-Soup.-1-pot-simple-ingredients-quick-SO-satisfying.-Vegan-options.-minimalistbaker-lentils-glutenfree-soup-recipe-4.jpg" srcset="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/12/COZY-Tuscan-Style-Beef-Lentil-Soup.-1-pot-simple-ingredients-quick-SO-satisfying.-Vegan-options.-minimalistbaker-lentils-glutenfree-soup-recipe-4.jpg 1456w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/12/COZY-Tuscan-Style-Beef-Lentil-Soup.-1-pot-simple-ingredients-quick-SO-satisfying.-Vegan-options.-minimalistbaker-lentils-glutenfree-soup-recipe-4-200x300.jpg 200w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/12/COZY-Tuscan-Style-Beef-Lentil-Soup.-1-pot-simple-ingredients-quick-SO-satisfying.-Vegan-options.-minimalistbaker-lentils-glutenfree-soup-recipe-4-768x1152.jpg 768w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/12/COZY-Tuscan-Style-Beef-Lentil-Soup.-1-pot-simple-ingredients-quick-SO-satisfying.-Vegan-options.-minimalistbaker-lentils-glutenfree-soup-recipe-4-683x1024.jpg 683w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/12/COZY-Tuscan-Style-Beef-Lentil-Soup.-1-pot-simple-ingredients-quick-SO-satisfying.-Vegan-options.-minimalistbaker-lentils-glutenfree-soup-recipe-4-600x900.jpg 600w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/12/COZY-Tuscan-Style-Beef-Lentil-Soup.-1-pot-simple-ingredients-quick-SO-satisfying.-Vegan-options.-minimalistbaker-lentils-glutenfree-soup-recipe-4-680x1020.jpg 680w"/></figure>
<p>Next comes tomato paste for rich tomato flavor, then diced tomatoes and broth. We opted to add both dried basil and oregano for plenty of Italian-inspired notes. </p>
<p>Lastly, lentils and kale are stirred in for some added plant protein and fiber.</p>
<figure class="wp-block-image"><img alt="Using a wooden spoon to stir a pot of our Tuscan Beef and Lentil Soup" class="wp-image-50255" data-jpibfi-post-excerpt="" data-jpibfi-post-title="1-Pot Tuscan-Style Beef &amp; Lentil Soup" data-jpibfi-post-url="https://minimalistbaker.com/1-pot-tuscan-style-beef-lentil-soup/" data-jpibfi-src="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/12/COZY-Tuscan-Style-Beef-Lentil-Soup.-1-pot-simple-ingredients-quick-SO-satisfying.-Vegan-options.-minimalistbaker-lentils-glutenfree-soup-recipe-8.jpg" data-pin-description="COZY Tuscan-Style Beef &amp; Lentil Soup. 1 pot, simple ingredients, quick, SO satisfying. <h3>How to Modify </h3>
<ul><li>The recipe is written to include beef or bison. However, <strong>if vegan or vegetarian</strong>, feel free to omit the meat and double up on lentils or beans of choice.</li><li>In addition to lentils, we also tested this soup with <strong>white beans</strong> and thoroughly enjoyed it! Other kinds of lentils (such as red lentils) would also work well.</li><li>We opted for kale, but could also see <strong>other sturdy greens</strong>, such as collard greens, working well.</li></ul>
<figure class="wp-block-image"><img alt="Stirring fresh kale into a pot of our Tuscan Beef &amp; Lentil Soup" class="wp-image-50259" data-jpibfi-post-excerpt="" data-jpibfi-post-title="1-Pot Tuscan-Style Beef &amp; Lentil Soup" data-jpibfi-post-url="https://minimalistbaker.com/1-pot-tuscan-style-beef-lentil-soup/" data-jpibfi-src="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/12/COZY-Tuscan-Style-Beef-Lentil-Soup.-1-pot-simple-ingredients-quick-SO-satisfying.-Vegan-options.-minimalistbaker-lentils-glutenfree-soup-recipe-12.jpg" data-pin-description="COZY Tuscan-Style Beef &amp; Lentil Soup. 1 pot, simple ingredients, quick, SO satisfying. Vegan options. #minimalistbaker #lentils #glutenfree #soup #recipe" data-pin-title="1-Pot Tuscan-Style Beef &amp; Lentil Soup" sizes="(max-width: 960px) 100vw, (max-width: 1149px) 590px, 720px" src="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/12/COZY-Tuscan-Style-Beef-Lentil-Soup.-1-pot-simple-ingredients-quick-SO-satisfying.-Vegan-options.-minimalistbaker-lentils-glutenfree-soup-recipe-12.jpg" srcset="https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/12/COZY-Tuscan-Style-Beef-Lentil-Soup.-1-pot-simple-ingredients-quick-SO-satisfying.-Vegan-options.-minimalistbaker-lentils-glutenfree-soup-recipe-12.jpg 1456w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/12/COZY-Tuscan-Style-Beef-Lentil-Soup.-1-pot-simple-ingredients-quick-SO-satisfying.-Vegan-options.-minimalistbaker-lentils-glutenfree-soup-recipe-12-200x300.jpg 200w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/12/COZY-Tuscan-Style-Beef-Lentil-Soup.-1-pot-simple-ingredients-quick-SO-satisfying.-Vegan-options.-minimalistbaker-lentils-glutenfree-soup-recipe-12-768x1152.jpg 768w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/12/COZY-Tuscan-Style-Beef-Lentil-Soup.-1-pot-simple-ingredients-quick-SO-satisfying.-Vegan-options.-minimalistbaker-lentils-glutenfree-soup-recipe-12-683x1024.jpg 683w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/12/COZY-Tuscan-Style-Beef-Lentil-Soup.-1-pot-simple-ingredients-quick-SO-satisfying.-Vegan-options.-minimalistbaker-lentils-glutenfree-soup-recipe-12-600x900.jpg 600w, https://minimalistbaker.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/12/COZY-Tuscan-Style-Beef-Lentil-Soup.-1-pot-simple-ingredients-quick-SO-satisfying.-Vegan-options.-minimalistbaker-lentils-glutenfree-soup-recipe-12-680x1020.jpg 680w"/></figure>
<p>We hope you LOVE this soup! It’s:</p>
<ul><li>Hearty</li><li>Flavorful</li><li>Quick &amp; easy to make</li><li>Comforting</li><li>Customizable</li><li>&amp; Seriously delicious</li></ul>
<p>This would make the perfect quick, hearty weeknight meal. Top with our <a aria-label="go-to Cashew Parmesan (opens in a new tab)" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/how-to-make-vegan-parmesan-cheese/" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">go-to Cashew Parmesan</a> for the ultimate cozy dish! </p>
<p>This recipe is also <strong>ideal for meal prep</strong> as it reheats beautifully throughout the week and <strong>freezes well</strong>!</p>

<h2 class="wprm-recipe-name">1-Pot Tuscan-Style Beef &amp; Lentil Soup</h2>
<div class="wprm-recipe-summary">
<p>Hearty, 1-pot Tuscan soup with tomatoes, lentils, and ground beef. Quick and easy to make, big flavor, incredibly comforting. Naturally grain-free and gluten-free with vegan options included.</p> </div>
<div class="wprm-recipe-details-container">
<div class="wprm-recipe-author-container">
<span class="wprm-recipe-details wprm-recipe-details-name wprm-recipe-author-name">Author:</span> <span class="wprm-recipe-details wprm-recipe-author">Minimalist Baker</span>
</div>
</div>
<div class="wprm-recipe-details-container">
<div class="wprm-recipe-times-container">
<div class="wprm-recipe-prep-time-container">

<div class="wprm-recipe-total-time-container">

<div class="wprm-recipe-ingredients-container">
<h3 class="wprm-recipe-header">Ingredients</h3>
<div class="wprm-unit-conversion-container"><a class="wprm-unit-conversion wprmpuc-active" data-recipe="50288" data-system="1" href="#">US Customary</a> – <a class="wprm-unit-conversion" data-recipe="50288" data-system="2" href="#">Metric</a></div> <div class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-group">
<h4 class="wprm-recipe-group-name wprm-recipe-ingredient-group-name">SOUP</h4>
<ul class="wprm-recipe-ingredients">
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">1-2</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">Tbsp</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">neutral oil </span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes">(such as avocado oil)</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">1/2</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">large</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">white or yellow onion, diced</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">1/2</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">tsp</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">each sea salt and black pepper, DIVIDED plus more to taste</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">6</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">cloves</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">garlic, minced</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">1/4</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">tsp</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">red pepper flake </span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes">(omit for less heat)</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">1</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">lb.</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">ground beef or bison </span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes">(grass-fed, organic, pasture-raised whenever possible // if vegan, omit and double amount of beans listed below)</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">3</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">Tbsp</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">tomato paste </span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes">(plus more to taste)</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">1</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">15-oz</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">can diced tomatoes </span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes">(with salt, add with juices)</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">1</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">quart</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">chicken broth </span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes">(or sub beef // sub vegetable broth if vegan // 1 quart = 4 cups)</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">1</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">Tbsp</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">dried basil </span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes">(or sub fresh to taste)</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">1</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">Tbsp</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">dried oregano </span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes">(or sub fresh to taste)</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">1</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">15-oz</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">can white beans or lentils*, slightly drained </span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-notes">(double amount if making vegan)</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-amount">4</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-unit">cups</span>
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">kale (or other sturdy green), chopped </span>
</li>
</ul>
</div>
<div class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-group">
<h4 class="wprm-recipe-group-name wprm-recipe-ingredient-group-name">FOR SERVING <em>optional</em></h4>
<ul class="wprm-recipe-ingredients">
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">Freshly minced parsley</span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name"><a href="https://minimalistbaker.com/how-to-make-vegan-parmesan-cheese/" target="_blank">Vegan parmesan cheese</a></span>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-ingredient">
<span class="wprm-recipe-ingredient-name">Red pepper flake</span>
</li>
</ul>
</div>
</div>
<div class="wprm-recipe-instructions-container">
<h3 class="wprm-recipe-header">Instructions</h3>
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-group">
<ol class="wprm-recipe-instructions">
<li class="wprm-recipe-instruction">
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text"><p>Heat a large pot over medium heat. Once hot, add oil. Let heat 30 seconds. Then add onion and a healthy pinch each salt and pepper and sauté until soft and translucent (~ 4 minutes), stirring frequently. Then add garlic and red pepper flake and sauté 1 minute more.</p></div>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-instruction">
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text">Add beef or bison and use spoon to break into small pieces. Then season with another healthy pinch each salt and pepper. Stir and cook until meat is browned (~4-5 minutes).</div>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-instruction">
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text"><p>Add tomato paste and stir to combine. Then add diced tomatoes (with their juices), broth, dried basil, and dried oregano and stir. Add (drained) beans or lentils (both from canned*), season with another pinch salt and pepper, and stir.</p></div>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-instruction">
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text"><p>Once simmering, reduce heat to low, cover, and cook for about 10-15 minutes to allow the flavors to meld. Then taste and adjust flavor as needed, adding more red pepper flake for heat, tomato paste for tomato flavor / depth of flavor, salt and pepper to taste, or dried herbs to taste.</p></div>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-instruction">
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text">Add kale and one final pinch each salt and pepper, then stir. Cover and cook for a few minutes more, or until kale is wilted and green.</div>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-instruction">
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text"><p>Serve hot as is, or garnish with fresh minced parsley, vegan parmesan cheese, and red pepper flake (all optional).</p></div>
</li>
<li class="wprm-recipe-instruction">
<div class="wprm-recipe-instruction-text">Store cooled leftovers covered in the refrigerator up to 3-4 days, or in the freezer up to 1 month. Thaw from frozen before reheating. Reheat in the microwave or on the stovetop in a saucepan or pot over medium heat (covered) until warmed through. Add more broth or water as needed to thin.</div>
</li>
</ol>
</div>
</div>
<div class="wprm-recipe-video-container">

<div class="wprm-recipe-notes-container">
<h3 class="wprm-recipe-header">Notes</h3>
<p>*If wanting to use dry lentils, you will need to increase cook time by ~15 minutes. Avoid adding kale until the lentils are done.<br/>*Nutrition information is a rough estimate calculated with avocado oil and grass-fed ground beef and without optional ingredients.</p>
</div>

<img alt="Avatar for Emily Fedele" class="avatar avatar-96 photo" height="96" src="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/fe6fa814bb73d919a55ca8d56e576932?s=96&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g" srcset="https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/fe6fa814bb73d919a55ca8d56e576932?s=192&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x" title="Gravatar for Emily Fedele" width="96"><span itemprop="name">Emily Fedele</span> <span class="says">says</span> </img></p>
<p class="comment-meta"><time class="comment-time"><a class="comment-time-link" href="https://minimalistbaker.com/1-pot-tuscan-style-beef-lentil-soup/?t=1582403224#comment-861867">February 9, 2020 at 10:14 am</a></time></p> </header>
<div class="comment-content">
<p>This is on repeat this winter. It’s delicious, hearty, and makes enough for two nights of dinner at my house. It’s really versatile too. I’ve added in a bunch of other veggies (mushrooms, peas) and white beans when I’ve run out of lentils. It also freezes beautifully. One of the best soups I’ve made. Thanks, Dana!!</p>

<div class="comment-content">
<p>Delicious! We made this tonight with ground lamb and half the amount of broth (veggie) to make it more stew-like, but followed the rest of the recipe as written. It was quick, easy and so satisfying! This will be a go-to recipe from now on.</p>
<p>Great work and thanks for sharing!</p>

<p>Meal prepped this beautiful soup tonight and it came out amazing! I didn’t use beef- I subbed it for ground Beyond meat. Texture was still “meaty” and flavorful. Will definitely be adding this to our meal-prep rotation!</p>

				// Used by Gallery Custom Links to handle tenacious Lightboxes
				jQuery(document).ready(function () {

					function mgclInit() {
						if (jQuery.fn.off) {
							jQuery('.no-lightbox, .no-lightbox img').off('click'); // jQuery 1.7+
						}
						else {
							jQuery('.no-lightbox, .no-lightbox img').unbind('click'); // < jQuery 1.7
						}
						jQuery('a.no-lightbox').click(mgclOnClick);

						if (jQuery.fn.off) {
							jQuery('a.set-target').off('click'); // jQuery 1.7+
						}
						else {
							jQuery('a.set-target').unbind('click'); // < jQuery 1.7
						}
						jQuery('a.set-target').click(mgclOnClick);
					}

					function mgclOnClick() {
						if (!this.target || this.target == '' || this.target == '_self')
							window.location = this.href;
						else
							window.open(this.href,this.target);
						return false;
					}

					// From WP Gallery Custom Links
					// Reduce the number of  conflicting lightboxes
					function mgclAddLoadEvent(func) {
						var oldOnload = window.onload;
						if (typeof window.onload != 'function') {
							window.onload = func;
						} else {
							window.onload = function() {
								oldOnload();
								func();
							}
						}
					}

					mgclAddLoadEvent(mgclInit);
					mgclInit();

				});
